Anhui Provincial School Joint Conference Opposes He Lu as President of Anhui University

▲ Lacking both talent and moral integrity | Using a general strike as a threat

(Anhui News) Since the Provincial Government appointed He Lu as the acting president of Anhui University, slogans and declarations to drive He out have appeared within the university. Anhui University is seen as a school prone to trouble, with almost no semester passing without disturbances. The background to these disturbances often originates from outside the university. On the 14th, the Anhui School Joint Conference resolved to oppose He's acting presidency and submitted a request to the Provincial Government to quickly appoint a formal president, and sent a letter to Anhui natives abroad expressing their opposition, and resolved that if the Provincial Government did not appoint another president by August 20th, all secondary schools would go on strike. The letter from the conference to Anhui natives abroad is recorded below: Anhui Provincial University has only been in operation for three years, and its foundation is not yet solid. Unless someone with outstanding talent, character, and experience takes charge, it will be impossible to develop it. He Lu's talent is not highly regarded in public opinion, and his personal conduct is not meticulous. Since the Provincial Government extended its invitation, public opinion has been in an uproar (omitted). Therefore, it was resolved that we are ashamed to associate with him, and we have separately presented a request to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government to appoint another formal president to take over the school. Gentlemen, you are respected elders of our hometown and models for the scholarly community. We hope that you will all advocate for this in order to value the education of our hometown.

Guangxi University to Continue Operations

Guangxi University has been closed for two years since it opened in 1928 due to political instability. However, as the highest institution of learning for fostering talent in Guangxi Province, it is highly anticipated for resumption for the sake of the general youth. It is heard that the university president, Dr. Ma Junwu, has received repeated telegrams urging him to return to Guangxi to plan for the restoration of everything. Mr. Ma has now returned to Shanghai and stated that the university is now working hard on repairs and construction. It is determined to continue operations next semester, initially enrolling approximately 500 students in the first, second, and third grades of the preparatory course. Next year, it will begin offering undergraduate courses in Arts, Sciences, and Engineering. In addition to recruiting students in Wuzhou, Liuzhou, Guilin, and Nanning in Guangxi Province, it is also recruiting at the High School Department of Great China University in Shanghai to facilitate enrollment for Guangxi students. The time is expected to be in early August.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Organizes Education Plan for Wu County

The Wu County Education Bureau received an order from the Provincial Department yesterday, roughly stating: "According to the report and organization plan submitted by Yang Yuangui, the Provincial Department's local education administration inspection specialist, after inspecting the county, it was found that the county's education funds were approximately 90,000 yuan in deficit as of the end of the 19th fiscal year. If remedial measures are not taken quickly, bankruptcy will be inevitable. After reviewing the proposed reorganization plan, such as matching income and expenditure in the total budget, the various income items should be earnestly reorganized, the various expenditure items should be further tightened, and the unfunded items should be urgently raised to compensate for the new and old deficits and set up repayment plans. This is the most important part of the remedial policy and should be carefully considered and implemented by the Bureau Chief and the County Magistrate. The budget for the 20th fiscal year must be based on the total income of 629,806 yuan as originally planned. The various expenses must be clearly divided and compiled according to the available numbers, without any increases or decreases. All fixed temporary expenses, which are similar in nature to regular expenses, should be canceled. Substandard classes should be consolidated in accordance with the standards set by the Provincial Department. The establishment of social education institutions in the 20th year should be temporarily postponed, and attention should be paid to enriching the content of the existing institutions and improving their efficiency. The science laboratory should be handled by the Bureau Chief after careful discussion of the various items in the original plan and submitted for approval. Social education supervisors should be added immediately to take sole responsibility. The simplified elementary school system should be promoted in accordance with the actual needs of the county and the pilot area plan for compulsory education should be submitted for approval first. The central school system can be examined and handled in accordance with the general guidelines issued by the Provincial Department. The Bureau Chief is the person responsible for the implementation of the county's educational administrative staff. He must not avoid difficulties and must work hard to reorganize it so as to lay the foundation for permanent peace, which is what is hoped for. The Bureau Chief has been sincere in handling affairs in the past and will not be without merit in breaking down the old ways and reorganizing. He should continue to be encouraged to strive for efficiency and should not have any timidity. In addition to sending it separately, the original reorganization plan is copied in full for your compliance."

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Submits Results of Middle School Curriculum Provisional Standards Trial to the Ministry of Education (II)

▲ Geography

| Second Operational Requirements

(1) Teaching methods should emphasize guiding students to fill out and draw various maps. "Reason" The most important thing in studying geography is to be familiar with the terrain. If students can be guided to fill out and draw maps, they can become familiar with the actual situation and develop the ability to draw maps readily.

(2) Teaching methods should pay attention to newspapers. "Reason" 1. There are many changes in geography, even in terms of place names, there are often changes, for example, Fengtian is now Shenyang, and Constantinople is now Istanbul. As for international relations and new material constructions in various countries around the world, they are changing rapidly, so special attention should be paid to newspapers. 2. If we can pay attention to newspapers, then new geographical materials can be obtained from the negotiations and wars caused by the recovery of the China Eastern Railway. If we can carefully read the geography of Manchuria to the three eastern provinces while studying the China Eastern Railway issue, we will gain even more.

| Fourth Teaching Material Outline |

(1) The teaching material outline is not connected with the time allocation and is too flexible. "Reason" The teaching material outline is not connected with the time allocation and is too flexible. Having a standard is equal to not having a standard.

(2) World Geography Teaching Material: In addition to focusing on the six countries that have the most relationship with China, it seems that attention should also be paid to small and weak nations. "Reason" 1. The Prime Minister once instructed us that to achieve China's freedom and equality, we must unite with the nations in the world that treat us equally and fight together, so all small and weak nations should be regarded as having the same relationship as the six countries and should be given attention. 2. The land of small and weak nations is mostly the colonies of imperialists. The independence of the colonies will further lead to the collapse of the imperialists, so paying attention to small and weak nations is also paying attention to countries such as Japan, the United States, Britain, and France.

▲ Arithmetic

| First Objectives |

(1) The objectives of high school arithmetic should be added to cultivate students' habit of calmly solving difficult problems, so that they will not be afraid of difficulties and will not be discouraged by failures. "Reason" In addition to striving for practicality, high school students learning arithmetic should cultivate their courage to struggle and the spirit to solve difficult problems, so that they can pursue advanced academics or strive to serve the society.

| Second Teaching Material Outline |

(1) In the high school arithmetic outline, under the item of equation groups in algebra (B), a general theorem and application of determinants should be added. "Reason" Determinants are a general method for solving general linear equations. They must be applied in analytic geometry and are widely used, so they should be taught.

(2) Regarding the geometry D. Quadratic curves, it seems that they should be deleted and merged into analytic geometry. "Reason" It is not easy to understand quadratic curves in Euclidean geometry, and it takes a lot of time. It is quite suitable to teach them in analytic geometry. Otherwise, if quadratic curves are taught immediately after solid geometry, it will not only be unclear, but it will also repeat the disadvantage of analytic geometry.

| Third Time Allocation

(1) The time allocation for junior high school arithmetic should be changed to the table below.

First Year Second Year Third Year

Weekly Hours Weekly Hours Weekly Hours

First Semester Arithmetic 5 Algebra 5 Algebra 2 Geometry 3

Second Semester Arithmetic 5 Algebra 3 Geometry 2 Geometry 5

"Reason" Using subject-based mathematics and allocating time according to regulations, in the first semester of the first year, there are 5 hours of arithmetic and in the second semester, there are 2 hours of arithmetic and 3 hours of algebra. However, the materials for arithmetic must be connected with elementary school arithmetic and expanded, and application exercises related to the knowledge and experience of daily life, such as abacus, must be inserted. Since there are many materials and the students' level is one year short of that of elementary school students, the situation is different from the past. In the first and second semesters of the first year of junior high school, both should be changed to 5 hours of arithmetic, and the basic concepts of algebra, positive and negative numbers, and simple equations should be foreshadowed when teaching arithmetic to introduce the path of algebra, so that the foundation is more solid and there is no disadvantage of half-baked, miscellaneous, and unspecialized knowledge. Therefore, in the first semester of the second and third years, algebra will be taught exclusively, and in the third year, algebra and geometry will be taught in combination, and in the third year, geometry will be taught exclusively, and trigonometry is planned to be taught in high school.

(2) High school arithmetic should be 20 credits. "Reason" According to the general table, high school arithmetic has 19 credits, and according to the sub-table, it only has 18 credits, so it is known that there must be an error in the middle. However, according to the trial results of the affiliated schools for three semesters, it is always felt that there is not enough time to complete the teaching material outline in the curriculum standards as scheduled. It is planned to set it to 20 credits and add one credit to trigonometry in the fourth semester and reduce one credit to analytic geometry. In the fifth semester, analytic geometry is changed to four credits.

| Fourth Operational Requirements 1

(1) In the operational requirements of high school arithmetic, the actual application of trigonometric surveying of nearby school areas should be added. "Reason" Surveying directly applies trigonometry for the construction work during the period of political tutelage. Paying attention to surveying when learning trigonometry is directly to promote the application of theory and indirectly to cultivate the skills to engage in a profession.

▲ Physics and Chemistry

| Second Time Allocation

(1) Minerals and chemistry should be taught separately. "Reason" It is difficult to find teachers who can teach minerals attached to chemistry, so they should be taught separately. However, this kind of separate teaching must be carried out at the same time so that they can be connected with each other.

(2) The teaching procedure for high school physics, chemistry, and biology should be regulated. "Reason" The teaching procedure for the three items of high school physics, chemistry, and biology has not been regulated. According to the trial results, it is most appropriate to teach biology in high school year one, chemistry in high school year two, and physics in high school year three.

| Fifth Teaching Key Points |

(1) High school physics, A, Original text, (1) Every week, the last fifteen minutes of the one-hour lecture should be used for demonstration experiments. It should be changed to every time a unit is taught, the beginning or the last fifteen minutes should be used for demonstration experiments. "Reason" Based on the experimental results, the teaching materials for physics cannot be completely taught in one hour. Therefore, there cannot be different performances every hour, and the final performance can prove the correctness of the theory. Starting the performance can use curiosity to arouse research interest, both of which should be adopted separately. (2) High school physics original text, (3) One hour should be spent every week on questions and answers or exams. It should be changed to one hour should be spent after each chapter is taught on questions and answers or exams. (Reason) Only three hours are taught every week. If another hour is spent on exams and Q&A, the lecture time will only be two hours per week. It is not only difficult to complete the prescribed teaching materials, but also there are too few exam materials, and it is difficult to get a systematic concept when held in fragments.

▲ Zoology and Botany

| First Time Allocation |

(1) Junior high school zoology and botany should be increased by at least one credit. "Reason" The original time allocation for junior high school botany and zoology was three credits each. After trying to teach according to the prescribed teaching material outline and teaching methods, I always felt that there was not enough time. If you want to reduce the teaching materials to fit the time, the prescribed teaching materials are very appropriate and should not be cut. Therefore, according to the experimental results, at least one credit should be added to each, that is, a total of eight credits. (End)

The decision on the results will be made tomorrow. It is feared that it will be difficult to recruit enough new students and a second entrance exam for new students will be held in mid-August.

Records of the Jiangnan Track and Field Team's Northern Expedition (3)

丨Five Days in Tianjin丨

During their five days in Tianjin, the Jiangnan Track and Field Team was warmly welcomed by the Tianjin sports community and highly regarded by Mr. Zhang Boling. The team's activities in Tianjin are described below.

▲Good Weather Suddenly Returns

▲Day One: Continuous rain had left the field muddy and unsuitable for competition, leading to discussions among Tianjin sports officials about the team first traveling to Liaoning when they arrived last night. However, no decision was made. Unexpectedly, on the first morning, the weather dramatically improved, with sunshine streaming through the windows while the team members were still deep in slumber. The proposal to first go to Liaoning was therefore abandoned. Apart from a light workout at the Nankai Middle School sports field at 4 p.m. that afternoon, no other activities took place.

▲The Beautiful Scenery of Nankai

▲Day Two: At 9 a.m., Mr. Zhang Jiwu dispatched a representative to guide the entire team to visit Nankai University in Balitai. Balitai used to be a desolate area in the southern suburbs of Tianjin, overgrown with reeds and neglected. Now, thanks to Mr. Zhang Boling's tireless efforts, Nankai University has been built, including the Science Hall, Library, Showshan Hall, and dormitories for both male and female students, all completed one after another. It is not only the highest institution of learning in the North, but Balitai has also become the only famous scenic spot in Tianjin in less than ten years. The layout of Nankai University resembles a large park, with dense shade and a variety of flowers, creating a sense of contentment that makes one reluctant to leave. This contributes to the positive academic atmosphere at Nankai. The university is surrounded by rivers, making boating possible. In the eyes of Tianjin residents, it is akin to West Lake in Hangzhou or the Three Seas in Beijing. Every evening, one can find Chinese and foreign men and women boating for leisure, making it a key social venue in Tianjin. After touring the campus, the team members boarded four boats and cruised around the scenic spots. They then disembarked at Haiguang Temple and attended a luncheon hosted by the Tianjin Sports Association. During the luncheon, Mr. Zhang Jiwu, Chairman of the Tianjin Association, and Mr. Zhang Boling, Chairman of the National Sports Association, delivered speeches, emphasizing that the visit of the Jiangnan team was intended to promote track and field sports and inspire similar enthusiasm throughout the country. Finally, team leader Wang Fudan gave a speech of thanks, and the event concluded. At 4 p.m., the team conducted a formal practice session at Nankai Middle School, attended and photographed by reporters from various newspapers.

▲Zhang Boling Hosts a Welcome Banquet

▲Day Three: Preparing for the competition against the Tianjin team tomorrow, the team rested completely. Team members were not allowed to leave. Mr. Zhang Boling personally hosted a luncheon to entertain the team.

▲Day Four: Starting at 4 p.m., the team competed against the Tianjin team. Detailed information has already been reported in the newspapers.

▲Day Five: The team departed for Beijing on the 9 a.m. train.

The Decline of the Honolulu Overseas Chinese Baseball Team, a Foundation of Chinese Baseball

The Chinese people pay little attention to baseball, which leads to frequent failures in the Far Eastern Games. The Chinese expatriate community in Honolulu has extensively researched baseball techniques for over two decades. They have consistently maintained the Honolulu city championship, earning a well-deserved reputation in the Americas. At the 8th and 9th Far Eastern Games, Mr. Wang Zhengting, a pioneer in Chinese sports, specially recruited the team to represent the motherland. They secured second place in both Games, somewhat improving China's international standing in baseball. In 1928, the team defeated Keio University, the Japanese national champion, indicating their strength. In the last Far Eastern Games, the Japanese still feared the Honolulu team and lost to them despite fielding a national all-star team. However, the Honolulu team was stronger than any individual Japanese university team, as they could defeat Keio, Waseda, Meiji, and Hosei Universities, but slightly inferior to the Japanese national all-star team. However, the team members have aged, and their practice has become infrequent, leading to a significant decline in their skills. On the 12th of this month, the Meiji University baseball team from Japan traveled to Honolulu and held an international baseball match between China and Japan. Ten thousand spectators attended. After fierce fighting, the overseas Chinese team suffered a crushing defeat of 1-12. Meiji is not particularly strong, ranking fourth among Japanese universities. The defeat of the overseas Chinese team shows a significant decline, shaking the foundation of Chinese baseball.

Finance: Highly Volatile Margin Trading Last Week

▲Fluctuations Driven by German Debt News

Margin trading continued its upward trend last week, but with increased volatility and numerous twists. Daily fluctuations of over ten taels were common, hovering around 740 taels initially and later breaking through the 750 tael mark. The situation was complex and inconsistent, with market sentiment wavering due to conflicting news about German loans and financial instability. The start of rollover trading on the exchange, with September prices higher than August, led short sellers to cover. Initially at 5 qian, the premium later rose to over 3 taels, putting pressure on many. It is reported that Guangbang, Hengxing, and long-term spot trading firms have not completed their rollovers. From August 1st, the exchange will examine the goods received in July, currently estimated at around 30,000 bars. August margin contracts initially rose to 750 taels early in the week. On Thursday (the 16th, the rollover day), the low was 730 taels and 7 qian, closing at 740 taels, up 11 taels from the previous Saturday. September initially opened at 739 taels and a half, suddenly falling to 32 taels and a half, and reaching 54 taels towards the weekend, a difference of 22 taels and 4 qian, resulting in 47 taels. The combined August and September contracts (during this week) saw a net increase of about 14 taels after deducting over 3 taels for rollover costs. Overseas silver markets fell, and Shanghai exchange rates also weakened by one and a half grades. Bank transaction prices also tightened, with Chinese merchants occasionally covering shorts, reportedly still holding short positions. Hedging increased margin trading. Transactions by firms such as Dalianbang, Wanxing, Shunli, Tongtaichang, and speculator Mr. Wu have been mainly sales recently, although they remain long. Due to a major client's absence, transactions by Guangbang Hengxing and Shengda have been limited. Daily margin settlements, initially at 40 taels along the usual rate

, with a minimum of over 30 taels, and finally over 40 taels. Spot bars saw constant buying interest from Tianjinbang, but this decreased yesterday and the day before due to rumors of the firm suspending business. Prices for futures contracts rose by over 13 taels to over 11 taels. Until the German debt issue is resolved, margin trading is expected to undergo significant changes. Securities: Bond Prices Fell by Around 3 Yuan Last Week

▲Erratic Fluctuations Throughout the Week

▲Transactions Reached Over 120 Million Yuan

The bond market in Shanghai last week saw extremely limited spot trading, with only 39,000 yuan traded throughout the week. 19 Customs bonds accounted for 13,000 yuan, with the remainder only in the thousands. The futures market remained active, with significant daily trading volumes in major bonds. Transactions reached 17 to 18 million yuan on Monday, Wednesday, and Saturday, and over 20 million yuan on other days. Total transactions for the week amounted to 122.2 million yuan, an increase of over 27.7 million yuan compared to the previous week. Although unified tax treasury bonds began trading on Wednesday, these bonds are still rarely traded, with only one transaction made for the July futures, and no transactions thereafter. 20-year Customs bonds were the most active, with transactions reaching 40.89 million yuan, followed by 20-year cigarette bonds at 22.23 million yuan, 19 Customs bonds at 14.43 million yuan, 9 Shan bonds at 12.955 million yuan, Disbandment bonds at 12.35 million yuan, and Reorganization bonds at 11.14 million yuan. Other bonds, such as Customs bonds at 2.325 million yuan, 96 bonds at 2.12 million yuan, 66 bonds at 1.715 million yuan, and 7-year bonds at 60,000 yuan, saw lesser activity. Unified tax bonds only traded 5,000 yuan. In terms of fluctuations, the market environment seemed less favorable than before due to slight changes in the political situation and rumors in the market. In addition, heavy selling by Northern firms created a weak market sentiment. Bond prices weakened early in the week, with 20 Customs bonds falling by 2 yuan, and 20 cigarette and 19 Shan bonds also falling by over 1 yuan. Tuesday saw a further decline of about 1 yuan. Wednesday saw cautious sentiment and the most stagnant prices. On Thursday, rumors of a military revolt in the Stone District triggered market panic, leading to heavy selling and sharp price declines, falling by as much as 2.5 to 3 yuan at the lowest point. On Friday, the market sentiment improved as the continuous decline had been excessive and the rumors proved to be unfounded. Investors took advantage of the low prices to buy, with strong demand. 19 Customs and 20 Customs bonds rebounded by 1.8 to 1.9 jiao, and Disbandment and Reorganization bonds also saw significant gains. On the final day of the week, the trend became more peaceful, with only 20 cigarette bonds falling by 1 yuan. Other price movements were minimal. Overall, prices fell by about 2 to 3 yuan compared to the previous week, with only 7-year and 66 bonds remaining relatively stable. The bond market appeared chaotic. Yarn and Cotton: Sharp Price Increases in the Yarn Market Last Week

▲Slight Retreat at the Weekend, Still Up by Two Taels

▲Spot Yarn in High Demand, Particularly for Northern Sales

Yarn prices rose sharply early last week, showing a trend of increasing prices. The boycott movement intensified, drawing in speculators. Buyers flocked to the market, and firms increased purchases in anticipation of future needs. Tianjin firms actively procured spot goods for inland regions, further fueling the market. Prices for yarn contracts surged, with an increase of about 4 taels on Tuesday. However, the market eased slightly after one merchant unexpectedly sold without price limits. Overseas yarn and cotton markets were calm, and gold prices remained stable. Towards the weekend, continuous selling by major players caused prices to retreat slightly. However, yarn contract prices were still up by two taels compared to the previous week. Total transactions for the week amounted to 341,800 bales. Spot yarn sales were brisk, particularly for northern markets, with 16, 14, and 20-count spot yarn being particularly tight. Market sentiment remained strong. Firms purchased a total of 20,665 bales throughout the week, with traders buying 4,100 bales. The highest purchase volumes by firm are listed below:

Cotton Market Lackluster Last Week

▲Difficult Situation for Both Bulls and Bears

▲Spot Cotton Virtually Stalled

The cotton market has been uninspired for the past week, tending toward a stagnant situation. Overseas cotton markets have also been indecisive, and although exchange rates have risen, domestic concerns about floods and damage to cotton crops in Shaanxi initially boosted sentiment. However, the weather soon cleared, and the lackluster performance of US cotton markets further dampened market enthusiasm. Spot cotton sales have been sluggish, with mills showing no purchasing interest. This has resulted in a difficult situation for both bulls and bears. Japanese firms continue to absorb forward positions, with significant volume. Cotton market movements will depend on the conditions of new cotton and US cotton. Prices for contract and old cotton have weakened due to a shortage of buyers. New cotton prices, held firm by Japanese firms, were slightly higher. Overall, prices for each month were close to the previous week, with a slight increase of 2.3 qian. Transactions totaled 258,900 dan. The source of cotton was 3,650 bales of Yao cotton, with US cotton volumes similar to the previous week.

Grains: Prices Softening in the Hexia Rice Market

▲Xin Zha: Few traders were present at the market this morning. Su-Chang premium grades and Zhongguan grades declined by 2 jiao. Kunshan and Jiangyin white rice were losing ground, with prices softening by 1-2 jiao. Purchases of Nanbang, Shipu, Chonggu, Hangchuan, and Xitang late rice were weak, with remaining stocks plentiful, prices declining about 1 chi. Lu-bu sharp rice sales were poor, with flat conditions. Glutinous rice saw no demand from wineries, with prices continuing to fall. Although some early rice had arrived at the docks, volumes were extremely low, with prices remaining at original levels. 20-30 boats from the West Road brought approximately 2,000 dan.

▲Nanjing: Supplies from various regions were still plentiful, approximately 10 boats. Sales in urban and rural areas were sluggish. Thick glutinous rice and second-grade rice declined by 2 jiao, with extremely quiet trading and bearish sentiment. Customer sentiment was affected. Although the arrival of thin rice was low, sales were slow, and prices also fell by 1-2 jiao. Foreign Lu-bu sharp rice was stagnant, with prices declining. General conditions were weak, with prices declining both overtly and covertly. Early rice was sold as it arrived, with prices unchanged. A telegram from Annam stated that 100,000 bags of foreign rice would be imported within a week, causing rice prices in Shanghai to steadily decline.

Silk and Tea: Harvesting Mostly Stopped in Wuyuan Zi Tea Region

Wuyuan Zi Tea output has been very plentiful this year. Competition among tea firms drove prices up, leading farmers to harvest and process as much as possible, hoping to meet the demand. However, news of falling green tea prices in Shanghai soon spread, and firms lost interest. Cautious firms, even if they had not filled their quotas, were reluctant to buy more, causing prices to fall. Farmers in the northern mountainous regions, where tea output is highest, have stopped harvesting due to low prices and limited sales. However, Wudong Zi Tea continues to be harvested and sold, as demand from firms in the eastern regions remains strong, with prices hovering between 60 and 65 yuan, without declining.

Tunxi Seed Tea Merchants Need Much

Due to insect damage to the spring tea in Tunxi this year, the tea production in Shexian County suffered a reduction. Most merchants did not meet their purchase quotas. Everyone hopes for a bumper harvest of seed tea to make up for the shortfall. Therefore, as soon as the seed tea came onto the market, the merchants rushed to buy it as much as possible. Furthermore, the superior Zhenmei tea was transported to Shanghai, as the first Tunxi tea to arrive would fetch the highest price, making the merchants even more enthusiastic. Recently, tea merchants in Tunxi opened their price lists for lower-quality stored tea, with prices still around fifty or sixty yuan. There is a high demand for seed tea leaves of fine and tender quality, with asking prices remaining at sixty to seventy yuan. Many tea merchants are collecting from tea farms and rushing to Tunxi to sell. However, in recent days, the supply from the tea-growing areas has been gradually decreasing, and the quality of the leaves is deteriorating daily, with most tea farmers ceasing picking. It is said that the seed tea market will not last much longer.

Sugar Market: Japanese Sugar Plummets Due to Boycott

▲Coarse Granulated White Sugar Increases by Half a Penny and is Strong

Yesterday, the guild’s listed price for No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar (Dutch sugar) was well-received. The opening price was 11 taels and 4 qian. Fine granulated white sugar was 11 taels and 4 qian and a half. Later, coarse granulated white sugar rose to 11 taels and 4 qian and a half. The market was quite lively. No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was 11 taels, and slightly lower quality was 10 taels and 9 qian, with a bullish trend. Taikoo’s cube sugar B mark was 12 taels, CW mark was 11 taels and 8 qian, and HM mark was 11 taels and 3 qian. There was an extreme shortage of goods leaving warehouses, and the market was very lively. Wah Shun Company offered 1,000 bags of B mark at 12 taels, and also sold several hundred bags of coarse granulated white sugar at 11 taels and 4 qian. As Ningbo telegraphed that Japanese sugar shipments had stopped, and Shanghai was intensifying its economic severance with Japan, market sentiment weakened, and more goods were leaving warehouses. Buyers, anticipating potential issues with transportation and delivery, mostly took a wait-and-see approach, leading to sluggish transactions and a slight market decline. N mark was priced from 11 taels, 2 qian to 1 qian and 7.5 fen, SH mark was 11 taels and 0 qian and 7.5 fen, T mark was 11 taels, 6 qian and 2.5 fen to 6 qian, YT mark was 11 taels and 1 qian and a half, YRO mark was 11 taels and 0 qian and 5 fen, YP mark was 11 taels and 5 qian and a half, TK mark was 11 taels, 2 qian and a half to 2 qian, TM mark was 11 taels, 1 qian and a half to 1 qian, showing a weakening trend. The firm Zhen Xiang offered 2,000 bags of spot Hong Kong coarse granulated white sugar at 11 taels, 4 qian, and 2.5 fen per yuan, to be cleared in four days. The trade was very interested and the market extremely lively, with a strong upward trend.

Metals: Qingdao Merchants Buying Up 7.5-li Steel Plates

Yesterday, Qingdao merchants suddenly started buying up 7.5-li English steel plates, purchasing seven or eight hundred pieces. The market price was 6 taels and 5 qian per case, an increase of 1 qian and a half from before.

Tinplate from the East Rises Due to Boycott

Since the Wanbaoshan Incident, local merchants have been extremely indignant, leading to discussions of boycotting goods from the East, including tinplate, new lead wire, nails, coal shovels, and other items. However, the market price suddenly rose yesterday. Speculation points to hoarding by a small number of merchants. For example, 3'7" tinplate rose to 1 tael, 2 qian and 6 fen, and 3'6" tinplate rose to 1 tael and 3 fen, an increase of more than 3 fen from before. Nails and lead wire also increased by 3 to 4 qian each. Only merchants from areas along the Yangtze River were buying, with other merchants purchasing very little.

North-South Goods: Zhongxing Vegetables and Jinshan Branches Arrive Fresh

▲Price 19.5 Taels ▲68.5 Taels

The first batch of new Zhongxing vegetables arrived in Shanghai yesterday, totaling 391 packages, all independently sourced by various merchants. Samples were immediately displayed. Due to rain in the production area, the color was slightly inferior. Merchants from various regions inquired about purchases, with Guangdong merchants making the most transactions, at a price of 19 taels and a half. Approximately half has already been sold. If the arriving goods were dry and bright yellow, the selling price could have been higher. Unfortunately, the inferior color due to rain prevented a lively market. However, it is expected that they will be sold out by Monday.

Genuine new Jinshan branches arrived at a northern merchant's house yesterday, with 20 cases of Liansheng brand. The quality was mediocre. However, the weight was only about seven or eight piculs, so the asking price reached 68 taels and a half, more than 20 taels higher than old stock. Although this year's harvest is poor, the market price is too high, reducing consumption. Whether the market can stabilize in the future depends on sales.

Free Talk

World Anecdotes

— Hai Ke

Seventeen-Year-Old Hen that Lays Eggs

In Skipton, Yorkshire, England, there is an old hen that has broken the world record for egg-laying. It has been laying eggs for seventeen years since it came into the world. Therefore, everyone calls it "Old Lady." "Old Lady" is extremely fertile and has been laying eggs for seventeen years without fail. When its owner brought it home eleven years ago, he did not expect it to lay eggs, only wanting it to sit on duck eggs to hatch ducklings. Who knew that after the ducklings were born and went into the water, it would start laying eggs itself. Since then, it has been laying eggs every year from mid-April, always for six or seven weeks continuously, then resting slightly before continuing to lay eggs for another six or seven weeks. It is said that during its busy period, it lays an average of three eggs per week. If calculated over seventeen years, the number is quite considerable.

Special Treatment for Insomnia

A special method for treating insomnia has recently been invented by P. Boyd, a British genealogy expert. He is a member of the Genealogical Society. Some time ago, he suffered from insomnia, feeling mentally exhausted and in great pain. On the other hand, he began to compile a table of marriage names and detailed explanations from England and Wales between 1538 and 1837. He has already compiled 1.4 million entries in 139 volumes. No matter whose wedding date it is, it can be investigated clearly in just five minutes. He has to refer to no less than thousands of records, some of which are difficult to read due to their age. Every day, the incoming mail is also endless, supplementing and adding information, which is very troublesome. Boyd himself thinks that this work cannot be completed in less than a hundred years. Because it is too troublesome, he immediately became sleepy. As a result, his insomnia was completely cured.

Nuns of Nanxun

— A Xiang

Nanxun, a major town in western Zhejiang, has many nuns. Gentle and charming, their fame spreads throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River. There is much charm and interest in them. I will record some of it to serve as a page in the scandalous history of the Buddhist gate.

The best among them is Doumu Convent, located near the Nanxun Rainbow Bridge. The women there are known for their beauty and youth. In the past, the New Stage Theater once produced a play about it called "Doumu Convent." Someone was secretly sent to Nanxun, and the convent head was bribed with a large sum of money to lead the nuns to Shanghai to show their beauty on the stage. Just as their charms were about to be revealed, they were stopped by powerful forces, and it did not happen.

There is an event similar to "The Jade Dragonfly." It is said that a certain civilian from out of town accidentally entered a small convent in the western region. He mistakenly entered paradise, delighting the nuns. He engaged in tantric practices within the Buddhist texts. The man was not made of indestructible vajra. In less than a month, Shen Guisheng was consulted about him in the underworld. This tale of grief and charm is still used as conversation material.

Many Nanxun nuns keep their hair long, wearing new styles of chignons like ordinary women. In the sixteenth year of the Republic (1927), a certain old youth, angered by their lack of nun-like or lay-like behavior and their shameful unseemliness, gathered some like-minded people and sharpened their scissors, intending to shave their heads and make them all bare like Niu Mountain, to distinguish them from ordinary people. When the nuns heard the news, they were unwilling to sacrifice their black hair to the sharp blades of Bingzhou. For a time, it was chaos, with nuns escaping over the walls like butterflies and red apricots. Those who had protectors sought refuge under their protection, while others simply left the convent and went down the mountain to become courtesans. Due to this incident, the nuns of Nanxun declined slightly. Previously, an article in this journal by Mr. Chi Fo stated that the nuns of Nanxun were mostly young and beautiful, suitable for offering wine and captivating souls. This was three or five years ago. Now, the convent is still there, but the people are different. Those who open the door to receive guests are mostly old with wrinkled skin and white hair. If Mr. Liu visits again, he will be filled with emotion at the changes.

New Uses for Talking Pictures

— Geng Xin

Since the prevalence of talking pictures, not only are the figures in the play portrayed visually, but also audibly. When we are in the theater, it is as if we are talking in the same room with the people in the film. Recently, it was heard that the Illinois Supreme Court in the United States is considering using talking pictures to try cases. This has been submitted to the local bar association for consideration. According to Mr. Li, the president of a certain law school in Chicago, the court should use the new contributions of modern science to seek perfection in the performance of its duties. Using talking pictures to try cases can preserve the voices, appearances, attitudes, and actions of both parties and witnesses when they give their testimony without missing any details. Compared to only using printed or written records, it is naturally easier to achieve the goal of fairness.

A Record of a Bountiful Birthday Banquet

— Zhu Jue

The famous Sichuan painter Zhang Shanzi celebrated his fiftieth birthday with a banquet at Tao Le Chun. Over a hundred members of the Shanghai press, literary figures, and artists attended, enjoying music, wine, and elegant attire. I was fortunate enough to attend this grand event. I will record what I saw and heard, though the event may be past, I will still gather the fragrant grasses from the horizon.

▲Zeng Nongran's Painting of Pine Trees There were many paintings presented for his birthday on the walls, such as Wang Yiting's portrait of Shanzi, Xie Gongzhan's seasonal flowers, He Tianjian's ink landscape, Ma Wanli's pine tree, a collaborative painting of pine and crane by Ye Weishen, Zhang Yuguang, Wang Zhongshan, Gao Shangzhi, and others, Wu Yifeng's blue-green landscape, Xiong Songquan's pine monkey, and Cai Yimin's bamboo, all selections of the time. However, Zeng Nong Lao's ink pine tree was the most unique and clever. This painting by Nong Lao was created in the year of Yichou. The sparse, short pine tree is extremely crooked and proud. The inscription reads, "Zhang Dafeng's wrist moves like clouds and shakes feathers in the sky, closely resembling Lao Ran." With a smile, "In the fifth month of Yichou, the heat was unbearable and I couldn't sleep. I got up at night to create this." Nong Lao passed away, and this painting was treasured by his family. This time, Madame Zeng specially gifted it to Shanzi as a song of pine and cypress from a disciple. Shanzi calls his studio Dafengtang, and the inscription mentions Zhang Dafeng. Shanzi's birthday is in the fifth month, and this painting was also created in the fifth month. As if there were a predestined relationship with Zhang, the style and meaning of the master's school and the karmic connection with brush and ink make it a treasure indeed.

▲Gift of Painted Fans During the banquet, silk fans were given as souvenirs. One side of the fan featured a printed image of Shanzi's tiger painting, with grass and bamboo added and colored by Daqian. The other side featured Mr. Wenxiu, Shanzi's fourth younger brother, handwritten two chapters of Shanzi's self-descriptive poem for his fiftieth birthday. The calligraphy was exquisite and elegant. The poem and painting were a perfect match. The guests could carry them in their sleeves, embracing the style of Dafengtang and enjoying themselves immensely.

▲Harmonious Poems Many poems were written in response to Shanzi's two self-descriptive poems, filling the walls with beautiful verses. Wei Ruosou's rhyming and Wang Menggong's rhyming collection of sentences were particularly excellent. Wei's poem says: "Both are wanderers, living by the seaside. Forget distinctions, see poverty. Black and white eyebrows are similar, the body is pure in painting. The moss and lichen now agree, and I have long respected your kinship. The spirit of the tiger is fierce, in the vast valleys. Wonderful in the place of clear history, revealing the leisure of an official. Painting on reeds inherits the jade room, the hibiscus supports the island mountain. A song of pine and cypress, I cannot delete it." Wang's poem says: "When the sea flows horizontally, I move my home near the sea. Friends are many and good, laughter can cure poverty. You excel in painting in poetry, I am ashamed that my learning is not pure. Climbing the hall to celebrate your birthday today, colorful clothes are peaceful and intimate. The belly contains a thousand years of achievements, leisurely between heaven and earth. Talent is high and far from the vulgar, ambition is great and cannot be stopped. Yi Yi is famous in the world, I think of buying a mountain. Writing books to enjoy the years, do not lightly delete the world." Wang's poem is a collection of sentences, but it is completed in one breath, seamless. As the ancients said, "Literature is born from heaven, and wonderful hands obtain it by chance."

Random Musings on Korea (10)

— Ji Ping

After a week in Seoul, I headed to Pyongyang, the former capital of Korea and now the second-largest commercial port on the peninsula. (Note: This was the place where the anti-Chinese riots by Japanese and Korean vagrants were most violent, and where Chinese compatriots suffered the most deaths and injuries.) There were twelve of us traveling together, the renowned Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team on a tour of the East. Unexpectedly, there were over two thousand compatriots waiting to greet us at the station. They each held the national flag of the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Crimson Ground, shouting "Long live the Republic of China" three times. This enthusiastic and sincere display of emotion made us truly "feel overwhelmed by favor." Moreover, besides the Chinese merchants, most of them were strong and sturdy farmers and laborers in short shirts and bare feet, their faces filled with joy. No wonder the Japanese and Koreans were also gathered in crowds to witness this unprecedented grand event of Chinese people. In the evening, they gathered again at the Zhonghua Building for a welcome party. It is said that this was the first meeting between the Korean Chinese community and the domestic sports circles. They hoped that athletic groups would come to Korea often to bring them honor and that Chinese planes and warships would come to console them and fight for the dignity of the Chinese. They reported the suffering they had endured in Korea, word by word, expressing a united desire and fervent hope for the unification and strengthening of the motherland. That the laboring class could awaken on their own is indeed a very good sign.

Pyongyang is the battlefield of the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95. There are many historical sites, such as Xuanwu Gate, Mudan Terrace, Choisung Terrace, Eulmil Terrace, and the historically significant Tomb of Gija. After paying our respects, we were awakened with a jolt, filled with the poignant feeling of "it's unbearable to look back on those years." During the Sino-Japanese War, our army defended the west of the Daedong River, while the Japanese army concentrated on the east. The two armies confronted each other. Qing General Zuo Baogui was trapped in Xuanwu Gate. Japanese General Harada Jūkichi led sixteen elite soldiers to attack at midnight, breaching our defenses. As a result, the entire army retreated in disarray towards Andong. With the loss of Pyongyang, our army's base in Korea was completely plundered by the enemy. Mudan Terrace is on the summit of a mountain. The remains of the strong fortifications built by our army still exist. Choisung Terrace was originally called Oseung Terrace. It was renamed after Japan annexed Korea to signify the glory of their victory. A wooden sign stands a few steps in front of the terrace, depicting the battle formation and marking the routes of the Japanese Asaning Detachment and Wonsan Detachment's sneak attacks on our army's first to fifth fortresses. Eulmil Terrace was originally guarded by our General Ma Yukun. He retreated after the Xuanwu Gate was breached. Ancient trees nearby reach the sky. Looking at the bullet holes on the trees, dense as a honeycomb, one can imagine the intensity of the battle between the two armies thirty-six years ago. Various steles and plaques have all been changed from Chinese to Japanese to highlight their glory and expose our national humiliation. Seeing this, those with a conscience feel even more disheartened and heartbroken. The Tomb of Gija is where Gija of Zhou was enfeoffed in Korea and later buried. Recalling Gija's achievements three thousand years ago, how can we comfort his heroic spirit? This proves the long and profound historical relationship between China and Korea. And now, we allow those dwarfish slaves to run rampant. Floating on the Daedong River, we can only hear the "hatred of a lost nation."

In short, Japan's ambition to plot against us is a consistent action from top to bottom. Our four hundred million compatriots should also be awakened. Regarding the tragic anti-Chinese incident in Korea, we have always believed that the Koreans were acting under duress and are not our negotiating counterparts. However, we must not forgive Japan's premeditated conspiracy. We pledge to support the government as a backing, conducting serious negotiations. Our minimum demands are: (1) Strictly punish the instigators of the anti-Chinese riots by Japanese and Korean vagrants. (2) Compensate all losses suffered by Chinese immigrants. (3) Provide relief to the deceased and injured Chinese immigrants. (4) The Japanese government issues a written apology to the Chinese government. (5) Guarantee that the same incident will never happen again. Until the negotiations achieve their goals, the whole nation must unite with a resolute and courageous spirit to permanently sever economic ties with Japan. I believe that if we persist in this effective boycott for more than six months, Japan will definitely soften.

Finally, I would like to inform the readers that this article was originally part of my "Scraps from a Trip to the East." Written in a rambling manner, it is published here first. The motivation is entirely driven by righteous indignation over the Korean incident. I hope readers will forgive any errors. (The End)

Rotary Club Fiction

??? (27)

— Xu Zhuodai

Zi Liang looked in the direction she pointed and saw a white voile long gown hanging on the coat rack. He quickly grabbed the sleeve and asked her,

"Is it this?"

"Yes! Don't go near it, I'm terrified."

As she spoke, she covered her eyes with both hands, not daring to look. Zi Liang quickly took down the gown and tossed it into the closet.

"Look! The ghost has been banished!"

The woman took her hands away from her eyes, still screaming in fright,

"There's still a big head!"

"Nonsense! That's my straw hat!"

Saying that, he took down the straw hat, wanting to take it to her to see, but she was too scared to look. Zi Liang tapped the top of the hat with his finger. Hearing the sound, she finally believed him and dared to take a closer look at the hat.

"Where's the white ghost?"

"That was a white long gown!"

The woman heard this, half believing, half doubting. However, Zi Liang dared not take out the gown again and hang it on the coat rack for her to see. While she was still unsettled, the nanny had already brought up the congee and side dishes for the woman to eat. She held a plate and walked to the bed, looking for a place to put it.

"I'm not getting up. Put the plate on the edge of the bed!"

The nanny placed the plate. The woman used her chopsticks to taste the side dishes first. The nanny turned to look at Zi Liang,

"It's dark now. Go downstairs and eat!"

Zi Liang was about to go down when he looked at the woman.

"I can't leave!"

Zi Liang stopped in his tracks.

"If you leave, I'll be scared again."

"I haven't had dinner yet!"

"Why don't you keep me company and eat congee with me?"

Youth Corner

Dean of Discipline

— San Mu

Our school's Dean of Discipline, Mr. Xi, is a student from a certain university. He seems to be about twenty-five or twenty-six years old. His face is dark with a hint of yellow, and his eyes are always tired. He wears a set of yam-colored Western-style clothes. He teaches Party Principles in our class. Whenever he enters the classroom, the students' spirits are immediately lifted, because after taking attendance, he doesn't teach from the book. First, he talks about the problems of youth's depression, then he rambles on about free love. Finally, he tells the students, "If you have any personal problems, feel free to talk to me individually. I will definitely point you to a way out. Don't think that just because I am a man, you shouldn't be embarrassed to talk…"

The classroom is as noisy as a restaurant. Everyone is talking to each other.

"Mr. Xi must be heartbroken."

"No, he has a mental illness. Don't you see that he always speaks incoherently? I heard that his wife is too unfashionable, and he often gets angry at her, so he is now mentally unstable…"

"Every time he complains to us, he is hinting at Ah Huan (a classmate). Don't you see that he is secretly looking at her with his eyes…"

Time passes quickly. Mr. Xi hasn't even started lecturing about the book.

The ringing of the bell vibrates in everyone's hearts.

Half a year of Party Principles class has been spent in tasteless conversation. Two weeks before the summer vacation, Mr. Xi saw that only five pages of the textbook had been taught, and he began to panic. When he came to class, he didn't even take attendance. He opened the book and read like a machine gun. He had to read at least ten pages before putting down the book and lecturing,

"In recent years, China has been oppressed by imperialism, so the late Premier created the Three Principles of the People to overthrow imperialism."

"Imperialism uses despotic means to oppress weak nations."

"Our nation is like a heap of loose sand, lacking a spirit of unity, so it is most easily invaded by imperialism. We young people must unite to overthrow imperialism. At the same time, to realize the Three Principles of the People, we must first overthrow imperialism…"

"Ah, how can you be sleeping…" Mr. Xi was lecturing enthusiastically when he suddenly felt that the classroom was too quiet. He happened to look down and saw several students slumped on their desks.

"Fine, I put in so much effort to lecture you, but you don't listen attentively. I'm not happy to lecture anymore."

"No, teacher, please lecture. We are listening very attentively."

"Teacher, you are really suffering too much. You should rest a bit in this hot weather. Anyway, class is about to end. There's no need to lecture."

"No, this is not right. This little book hasn't been finished in half a year. I feel very sorry to all of you. Now I want to work hard to make up for your Party Principles." After saying a few words of repentance, Mr. Xi cleared his throat again,

"From what has been said above, we can know that the only task of the Kuomintang now is to overthrow imperialism."

"If you don't have a book, you can share one with someone else." Mr. Xi noticed at a glance that there was no book on Hen's desk.

"It doesn't matter, teacher. Everything you say, I can remember in my heart. The book is too brief. It doesn't have as much about overthrowing imperialism as you lecture."

Mr. Xi was silent. The whole class burst into laughter.

One day, the weather was very hot. After Mr. Xi finished reading five pages, beads of sweat the size of beans couldn't help but fall. While reaching into his pants pocket with his right hand to take out a handkerchief, he walked to the door to close the classroom door.

"Teacher, what's the reason? It's so hot, why are you closing the door?" The students asked in surprise.

"I want to take off my coat. I'm afraid it would be unsightly for outsiders to see." As he said this, he took it off.

"Teacher, you are too selfish, harming everyone for your own benefit, making us hot."

"You are hot, but it's better than me. My clothes are made of thick wool."

"Then why did teacher have to wear a suit?"

"Wearing a suit has two advantages. First, it's convenient for walking and getting on the tram. Second, it easily shows the spirit of youth."

"Isn't wearing a Zhongshan suit the same?"

"Yes, I heard that teacher is still a member of the party. He should wear a Zhongshan suit even more, to show off his spirit and go overthrow imperialism."

Hahaha—echoed with a burst of laughter. Mr. Xi played deaf and dumb.

Once, Ni lost fifty yuan from her suitcase. When Mr. Xi heard about it, he immediately flew to the dormitory to search.

"How can a male teacher search a female student's dormitory? Isn't there a female disciplinarian?" A hot-blooded student was a little angry when she saw Mr. Xi's playful attitude.

"Whoever opposes, is a suspect."

"If you don't allow opposition, then you have to do it properly. Could it be that fifty yuan can fit in a small powder box?" Originally, Mr. Xi was too inappropriate. He couldn't bear to let go of every item of the female students, so it's no wonder he provoked them to say this to him.

The class bell rang. The fifty yuan had not been found, so they had to go to class temporarily.

"It is most unfortunate that a theft occurred at the school. Today's incident has been searched for half a day without any results. The dean of studies and the principal are unwilling to help at all, saying to leave it to me to handle. I think all of you are high school students, and your character must be very cultivated. Of course, you would not do such a thing, so I would like to discuss with you about the solution to this matter. Do you have any good methods?"

"What good methods do we have? This matter is of course the responsibility of the disciplinarian." The student who opposed the male teacher searching the dormitory was retaliating.

"This matter is, after all, a matter for the school. Everyone should share this responsibility. How can you not have a spirit of cooperation at all?"

Page 18

"What cooperation or non-cooperation? These are all small things. Now is Party Principles class. Please teach us how to overthrow imperialism." Li, who was easygoing, ridiculed in a funny tone.

"You are really optimists. People are in a hurry, but you are unwilling to lend a hand." Mr. Xi was disappointed and had to get back to the subject,

"When capitalists become extremely strong, they form imperialism, so opposing capitalists is also a way to overthrow imperialism."

"………………………………"

The next day, Mr. Xi held a general assembly specifically to report the theft.

"It is very embarrassing for a theft to occur in the school, because everyone is an intellectual. How can they still do such a thing? However, it was not found in the dormitory yesterday. I think this is not only the fault of the thief, but also the negligence of the loser. Now that there is this sacrifice, it is giving you a very good lesson. From now on, be careful. If the same accident happens again, I will not be responsible."

"Could it be that my money was lost for nothing?" Ni said softly to herself.

"Strange, why didn't he search the janitors and nannies when he searched the female students' dormitories yesterday? Today, he said these few words and considered the matter closed?"

"The janitor is his godfather, and the nanny is his mother-in-law…"

"Don't talk nonsense."

Mr. Xi is sick. It is said that he is lovesick. The other party is a certain teacher who teaches handicrafts at the school.

Ladies and gentlemen, you all know about the various aspects of our school's Dean of Discipline. I hope you will also write about your Deans of Discipline for comparison. At the same time, you can also know what kind of talents the Deans of Discipline in schools are now.

In the Chemical Experiment Room

— Li Zunquan

He took an iron basin and placed it on the central floor of the chemical experiment room. He poured some potassium chlorate and sugar powder into it and mixed them evenly. Then he returned to a corner of the room, took out a bottle of concentrated sulfuric acid, and placed it flat on the table. He used a dropper – a glass tube used for eye drops – and sucked a little sulfuric acid, then dripped a few drops into the iron basin. In this way, the potassium chlorate caused a strong heat due to the action of the sulfuric acid, and the sugar powder placed with the potassium chlorate was carbonized and ignited. He used a piece of waste paper as a medium to light the alcohol lamp. He then placed the lamp – the alcohol lamp – under the copper kettle placed on the tripod. In less than three minutes, the water in the kettle was hot. He poured a cup, and while drinking, walked to the window.

He had used this method to boil water – when he woke up thirsty in the middle of the night and couldn't find a match – countless times. But this time, he recalled a past event. This may have been because he used an excessive amount of potassium chlorate this time, resulting in a loud explosion. Or perhaps it was because the same scenery touched his mood.

It was also such a scene, probably. Everything in the vast and boundless wilderness, except for a few twinkling solitary stars, and a faint light emitted from his chemical experiment room, nothing else. Nothing could be seen. Truly, there was only deathly desolation and silence.

He sat next to a writing desk near the window, his eyes fixed on the elastic rubber (Gutta Purcha) and other mixtures in the pliers pot placed on the alcohol lamp.

Because there was no gas pipe installed in the countryside, naturally, there was no talk of using a Bunsen burner – a Bunsen burner that could adjust the heat and generate heat suitable for the required amount – to heat it to a suitable temperature. So he waited, constantly removing the alcohol lamp to prevent the heat from getting too high.

"Zong," a very familiar voice came in from outside the window.

"Ah, Lan, why are you here at this time? Is there anything important? Are you here alone?" He looked outside in surprise, half welcoming, half refusing to ask her.

"Yes, please open the door."

"Um," he hummed as he went to open the door.

—Boom—……pat pat……—An explosive, cracking sound, followed by a burst of firecrackers, lit up the entire room, and at the same time, thick smoke filled the air, scaring her, who had just stepped in, onto him. He, who had experience with explosions – often having explosions and not taking them seriously – was also a little flustered and at a loss for what to do. Did he want to go outside? Then what about Lan? He could only maintain a calm attitude and say,

"Lan... you... don't be like this... let me go put out the fire..."

"……" She closed her eyes and simply leaned on his chest.

Fortunately, the fire went out on its own in a few seconds. But a large area of the ceiling had been blackened by the smoke and fire.

He watched the fire go out, his heart settled. He wanted to push Lan away, but he didn't know why, it was as if he couldn't bear to. He supported her, or rather, put his arm around her, and went to the sofa. He and she sat side by side. He comforted her,

"Lan, look, it's calm now." He saw that she had her eyes closed.

"Ah, what's going on..." She opened her two tearful eyes, and immediately closed them again.

"Fine… you're scaring me, why do you want to scare me, threaten me… like… this, is it beneficial to you… you don't want me to come, just explain it clearly, why, why do you want to tease me like this, are you satisfied now, I haven't done anything to offend you, why do you want to hurt me, kill me, if you want to kill, just kill me like this, I…" She was crying, really crying. He initially thought it was the thick smoke that was making her tear up, so he gently wiped them away for her. But at this moment he understood, and this unexpected remark made him anxious and flustered, more flustered than when he heard the explosion. He quickly pushed her away, showed a solemn attitude, and defended himself, stating that he was open and honest, and that he revered and loved her, explaining that it was because he was too careless that the chemicals exploded, assuming that he was wrong, and that there should be a possibility of forgiveness. Finally, he said even more, "...If it weren't for you, I definitely wouldn't have left that seat, at least, I would have suffered some damage, in any part of my body, I really, don't know how to thank you... " He said a lot of words, only getting a few irrelevant echoes from her. As for what was in her heart, did she believe his words, did she mean to act spoiled?

Even he himself didn't know – and even now, he still doesn't know.

This Year is a Year of Solar Anomalies

Sunspots Suddenly Rare

—Talks of Japanese Astronomers—

Kobe News, sunspots were discovered all over the sun three or four years ago, surprising humanity. Recently, the Kobe Marine Meteorological Observatory in Japan used a ten-inch telescope to observe. On the ninth of this month, only three spots were seen in the southeast of the sun. The image was photographed in a dark room. The larger one was about one minute, and the smaller one was about five tenths of a minute, faintly visible. In particular, nothing was seen during the two-star period from June 13th to 27th. Afterwards, it reappeared. According to the members of the solar observation department of the meteorological observatory, it will continue to decrease next year. According to Dr. Ueda Nō, Professor of Astronomy at the Faculty of Science of Sai Kyo University, the decrease in sunspots generally takes eleven years as the first period. The least amount was in 1923, so this time it is 1934. Judging from the period, although it is currently in the middle, it continues to show this phenomenon. The previous year, its example, especially continuing for ten days, is a rare phenomenon. This year is really a year of solar anomalies, but what kind of impact the decrease of sunspots has on the earth and the weather has not yet been determined. It is difficult to say definitively, but it is not a completely annual phenomenon, so the configuration of air pressure also has times when it is put under special conditions. In short, put it under the conditions of special changes in the weather, that is, in the year when there are more sunspots, the earth seems to be generally not hot, but in the year when there are fewer sunspots, there are cool places on the earth, and there are also places where it is particularly hot, so it is difficult to say that it is a principle, it is said.

Eight Women's Organizations Meet in Geneva

Seeking Opinions from Major Women's Organizations on the Nationality Issue of Women Marrying Foreign Men

Geneva News, an international league committee composed entirely of women recently met in Geneva. This is the beginning of the League of Nations having a women's committee. This committee is seeking opinions from major women's organizations around the world to resolve the nationality issue of women marrying foreign men, but it will be submitted to the League of Nations Assembly in September. This nationality issue is extremely complex. It is expected that the committee will not ask how it is resolved, but only take the fundamental position that women should not be discriminated against. After the final resolution of the League of Nations Assembly in September, an international conference will be convened to discuss an international convention to be observed. The committee convened this time is composed of two representatives from each of the following eight international women's organizations: 1. International Council of Women, 2. International Women's Reference League, 3. Women's International League for Peace and Freedom, 4. Inter-American Commission of Women, 5. Equal Rights International, 6. World Women's Association, 7. All-Asian Women's Conference, 8. International Federation of University Women,

Next Month in Denver, USA

Car Drivers are Responsible for Living Things

It is a Moral Issue, Not a Legal Issue, The Same Applies to Chickens as it Does to People

According to American reports, car drivers often have several questions, namely, "Does a chicken have the right to cross the road and obstruct the progress of a car? Does a chicken farmer have the responsibility to keep chickens within a certain area? Should a car driver be responsible for compensation if they run over a chicken?" Mr. Stogner, the motor vehicle supervision commissioner of the State of Connecticut, has recently answered these questions. He said that these questions are more a moral issue than a legal issue. The use of dangerous machines (referring to cars) contains the possibility of killing chickens, so of course it should be done carefully. Therefore, every car driver must pay considerable attention and caution to any domestic creatures. This is a clear moral responsibility. Generally, the regulations regarding cars and children on the road can be applied to living things, it is said.

European Countries Expand Rayon Sales

It is More Difficult to Export Silk

European News, European countries have high tariff barriers on silk, making it more difficult to export silk. However, rayon and cotton cloth do not have such barriers, and various countries are expanding their sales extremely fiercely. In countries such as England, France, and Germany, the lower middle class has a greater need for silk made in Czechoslovakia, it is said.

Pregnant Murderers are Exempted from the Death Penalty

British Parliament Passes New Law

London News, the British House of Commons recently passed a bill unanimously without debate or opposition, abolishing the death penalty (hanging) for pregnant murderers. In the future, the heaviest penalty for pregnant women who commit this crime will be life imprisonment. This new law is the result of public agitation over the Wessey case. Mrs. Wessey was sentenced to death for killing her nine-year-old child while pregnant. Later, she gave birth to twins, and the court declared a reprieve, it is said.

U.S. Government Promotes Merger of Two Major Petroleum Companies

Major Revision of the Anti-Trust Ban Policy: Related to Anti-Russian Movement

New York Dispatch: The merger of New York Standard Oil (capital of $434 million) and Vacuum Oil (capital of $128 million), which was previously not approved by the U.S. government due to conflict with anti-trust laws, will now be promoted after a decision to stop the appeal to the Supreme Court. This fact clearly indicates a major revision, or even a shift in direction, of the traditional American policy of prohibiting trusts. The superficial reason for approving the merger is to facilitate the control of oil production quotas in the U.S. oil industry, but it is related to the recent anti-Russian movement expressed by President Hoover's proposal to postpone war debt payments and ban the import of Russian goods under the pretext of forced labor. It can be generally seen that the Standard Oil system is at the forefront of opposing the dumping of Russian oil.

International Fisheries Conference

Eight Resolutions Adopted During the Meeting

Paris Dispatch: The International Fisheries Conference, which began on July 10th, is scheduled to last until the 26th. The resolutions that have been adopted are as follows:

1. Freshwater fish farming.

2. Oceanographic research.

3. Fishing boat engines.

4. Sales system.

5. Preservation of catches.

6. Handling of catches on board.

7. Research on fish farms.

8. Pearl cultivation.

Social News

Marshal Foch's War Diary from the European War

— Translated by Gu Angruo

The Allied forces had fought bitterly for four years, and were exhausted and hoarse. Added to these mental blows, morale was low, and combat effectiveness naturally weakened. Fortunately, the soldiers under our banner were prepared to sacrifice themselves to reverse the decline. Clemenceau and Lloyd George, in their positions as leaders of their respective governments, used their excellent perseverance to assist the war effort. President Wilson joined the battle late, but now eagerly hoped to help the war effort wholeheartedly with the strong power of the United States. The responsibility of the Supreme Commander lies in applying positive methods to shorten the crisis, paying attention to weaknesses, avoiding confusion, and quickly reversing the situation.

At that time, on June 5th, in order to prevent the enemy from attacking between Montdidier and Noyon, I transferred a division (the 14th Division) from the detachment on that front to General Pétain's command. I asked General Haig to study the problem of another division of British troops replacing this detachment.

I made various arrangements to avoid the disadvantage of the Allied forces only being able to parry without being able to retaliate. On one hand, I transferred the reorganized French divisions and the American troops arriving from the British side to the areas of Lorraine and Vosges. On the other hand, I transferred some French troops to the British line to prepare for the German offensive that could occur at any time in the area of the Somme and Arras. At the same time, I studied the possibility of launching an offensive north of the Somme and on the front line of the French Fifth Army in order to restrain the enemy's forces while taking a defensive stance on the Oise River.

Finally, as the decisive battle was about to begin, I wrote to the Commander-in-Chief of the French Army, telling him not to forget to base his actions on the operational plan, to achieve strategic results, to fulfill the various responsibilities of a commander, and to instill the appropriate spirit in all participating officers and soldiers.

After the artillery bombardment that began at midnight on June 9th, Commander Hutier's infantry reached our defensive line between the Avre valley and the Matz valley at 3:45 a.m. At 6:00 a.m., the enemy's attack extended to the Oise River.

The German forces were not evenly distributed along the line. The forces on both wings were scattered, while the forces in the center were concentrated between Lassigny and the Matz valley, undertaking the offensive with nine to thirteen divisions.

The Allied forces collapsed in the center. The French 58th and 125th Divisions retreated immediately upon contact. Around 7:00 a.m., they were driven by the enemy past Gury. Around

10:00 a.m., the enemy captured our second line, from Marie to Méry-la-Montagne, a length of seven and a half miles. The Saint-Claude plateau and the Matz forest also fell into enemy hands one after another.

Six divisions of the French reserves joined the battle, and fortunately, they thwarted the enemy's offensive in the afternoon. In the evening, the enemy stopped at the line of Marie, Belloy, Margny, and Vandélicourt.

In short, Commander Hutier's attack, except for the right wing where there was not much progress, had indeed broken through the French defensive line in all other directions. Compiègne was directly threatened.

But I believed that the strength of the reserve corps was still sufficient to cope with this situation. Moreover, the Bavarian Crown Prince's troops had not joined the battle on June 9th. I therefore decided not to move Haig's forces. However, as a precaution, I asked him to transfer a division from the southern part of the 22nd Corps to the vicinity of Conty on the morning of the 10th, and then to fill the gap south of the Somme with another division. This would enable General Pétain to deploy all of the French reserves behind the First Army.

On the 10th, the enemy continued to attack, but not as smoothly as the day before. Although the enemy added a fresh division to help the battle, he only gained some ground west of Méry. His only important progress was east of Méry, where the retreat of the French 53rd Division opened the door directly to the Ribecourt valley. The Germans were able to gain a foothold between Montmacq and Chevincourt on the right bank of the Oise River. However, the extension of German forces in this area threatened the retreat of the French forces (38th Corps) on the left bank of the Oise River to Barisis, Tracy-le-Val, and Pusy-la-Campagne, the old defensive line of 1914.

Despite this setback, the results of the 10th were generally satisfactory. "The enemy's advance was not as smooth as the several offensives since March. Our army is firmly holding its ground with a step-by-step defense. The reinforcements that have arrived can also be deployed appropriately." French defensive works, based on recent plans, are arranged both deep and solid, causing the enemy's sudden attacks under intense artillery fire to be frustrated and stopped.

Commander Fayolle is now preparing to launch a large-scale counter-offensive against the enemy's flanks with five fresh divisions, four divisions in the first line, taking advantage of the opportunity.

After the German army's third offensive in the spring of 1918, my important responsibility was to consolidate the current situation and plan for the Allied forces' future operations based on the lessons of recent battles.

Although we are extremely interested in past battles, the urgent needs of the current situation should be given priority. The enemy clearly will not be content with the setback in the Méry area. The enemy still has a strong reserve army. It is said that there were 54 divisions on June 15th, 61 divisions on June 20th, and 75 divisions on June 30th. Among them, the 55th division is a fresh force.

The enemy has made very smooth progress on the Somme, Flanders, Champagne, and Oise River fronts. Our army has suffered heavy losses. The enemy seems to have a need to take advantage of superior forces and advance victoriously. On the one hand, he must know that the United States will soon join the war with its unstoppable force. On the other hand, he must feel that the crisis that the British and French armies have already experienced is approaching him. (Note: In June 1918, the German Supreme Command had to call up soldiers of the 1919 class and new recruits of the 1920 class. Some were formed in May and could be sent to the front line in July).

Therefore, the enemy will soon launch a new offensive, but where will they attack? Although it is believed that he will attack the British line, we cannot ignore the possibility that large enemy forces may move against any section of the French line. Therefore, I decided that the Allied reserve forces should be prepared to move to the front line from the North Sea to the Vosges River at any time to assist the British or French forces in battle. Both the British and French armies must be fully prepared to meet the enemy. (To be continued)

Home
